You can download one in the app, or from www.kiwix.org in your browser. You *must* download an archive for this app to work properly: it only comes bundled with a small test archive (about a jazz musician) so you can get a feel for how the app works.\r\n\r\nIf you want the full English-language Wikipedia with images, you will need a *large* microSD card in your device, or plenty of disk space. The file is currently 77 gigabytes and you might want to download it using BitTorrent (torrent link provided in the app). However, if you have limited storage you can still download specific parts of Wikipedia, such as medical pages, maths or computing pages, or a no-pictures version which is 19 gigabytes.
